## Column Sizing<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-columnSizing" class="docs-header-icon"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>

<table class="_apiReference_1nt5n_20 _apiReference_119gq_18 no-zebra">
<tbody>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">setColumnWidths<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-columnSizing-setColumnWidths" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to setColumnWidths property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
Function
Sets the column widths of the columns provided. The finished flag gets included in the resulting event and not used internally by the grid. The finished flag is intended for dragging, where a dragging action will produce many <code>columnWidth</code> events, so the consumer of events knows when it receives the last event in a stream. The finished parameter is optional, and defaults to <code>true</code>.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">sizeColumnsToFit<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-columnSizing-sizeColumnsToFit" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to sizeColumnsToFit property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
Function
Adjusts the size of columns to fit the available horizontal space. Note: it is not recommended to call this method rapidly e.g. in response to window resize events or as the container size is animated. This can cause the scrollbar to flicker. Use column flex for smoother results. If inferring cell data types with custom column types and row data is initially empty or yet to be set, the column sizing will happen asynchronously when row data is added. To always perform this synchronously, set <code>cellDataType = false</code> on the default column definition.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/column-sizing/#auto-size-columns-to-fit-grid" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Auto-Size Columns to Fit Grid<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />ColumnAutoSizeModule</a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">autoSizeColumns<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-columnSizing-autoSizeColumns" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to autoSizeColumns property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
Function
Auto-sizes columns based on their contents. If inferring cell data types with custom column types and row data is initially empty or yet to be set, the column sizing will happen asynchronously when row data is added. To always perform this synchronously, set <code>cellDataType = false</code> on the default column definition.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/column-sizing/#auto-size-columns-to-fit-cell-contents" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Auto-Size Columns to Fit Cell Contents<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>

## Events<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-events" class="docs-header-icon"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>

<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">addEventListener<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-events-addEventListener" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to addEventListener property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
Function
Add an event listener for the specified <code>eventType</code>. Listener will receive the <code>event</code> as a single parameter. Listeners will be automatically removed when the grid is destroyed.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />EventApiModule</a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">

<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />EventApiModule</a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">addGlobalListener<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-events-addGlobalListener" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to addGlobalListener property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
Function
Add an event listener for all event types coming from the grid. Listener will receive <code>eventType</code> and <code>event</code> as parameters. Listeners will be automatically removed when the grid is destroyed. If handling multiple event types it is recommended to use <code>event.type</code> to enable TypeScript to infer the event parameters.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />EventApiModule</a></td>

<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">addRenderedRowListener<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-events-addRenderedRowListener" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to addRenderedRowListener property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
Function
Registers a callback to a virtual row. A virtual row is a row that is visually rendered on the screen (rows that are not visible because of the scroll position are not rendered). Unlike normal events, you do not need to unregister rendered row listeners. When the rendered row is removed from the grid, all associated rendered row listeners will also be removed. listen for this event if your <code>cellRenderer</code> needs to do cleanup when the row no longer exists.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/row-events/" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Row Events<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>

</tr>

</table>

<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">getColumnFilterInstance<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-filter-getColumnFilterInstance" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to getColumnFilterInstance property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>

Returns the filter component instance for a column. For getting/setting models for individual column filters, use <code>getColumnFilterModel</code> and <code>setColumnFilterModel</code> instead of this. <code>key</code> can be a column ID or a <code>Column</code> object.

<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">setFilterModel<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-filter-setFilterModel" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to setFilterModel property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
Function
Sets the state of all the column filters. Provide it with what you get from <code>getFilterModel()</code> to restore filter state. If inferring cell data types, and row data is initially empty or yet to be set, the filter model will be applied asynchronously after row data is added. To always perform this synchronously, set <code>cellDataType = false</code> on the default column definition, or provide cell data types for every column.

<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">destroy<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-miscellaneous-destroy" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to destroy property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
Function
Will destroy the grid and release resources. If you are using a framework you do not need to call this, as the grid links in with the framework lifecycle. However if you are using Web Components or native JavaScript, you do need to call this, to avoid a memory leak in your application.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">isDestroyed<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-miscellaneous-isDestroyed" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to isDestroyed property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
Function
Returns <code>true</code> if the grid has been destroyed.</td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">setGridAriaProperty<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-miscellaneous-setGridAriaProperty" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to setGridAriaProperty property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
Function
Sets an ARIA property in the grid panel (element with <code>role="grid"</code>), and removes an ARIA property when the value is null.<br />
<br />
Example:<br />
<code>api.setGridAriaProperty('label', 'my grid')</code> will set <code>aria-label="my grid"</code>.<br />
<code>api.setGridAriaProperty('label', null)</code> will remove the <code>aria-label</code> attribute from the grid element.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/accessibility/#aria-attributes" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">ARIA Attributes<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />RenderApiModule</a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">getGridId<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-miscellaneous-getGridId" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to getGridId property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>

<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">

Function

</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">isAnimationFrameQueueEmpty<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-miscellaneous-isAnimationFrameQueueEmpty" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to isAnimationFrameQueueEmpty property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>

<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
Function
Iterates through each node (row) in the grid and calls the callback for each node. This works similar to the <code>forEach</code> method on a JavaScript array. This is called for every node, ignoring any filtering or sorting applied within the grid. It is not called on any pinned row nodes. If using the Infinite Row Model, then this gets called for each page loaded in the page cache.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/accessing-data/#iterating-rows" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Iterating Rows<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />RowApiModule</a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">forEachNodeAfterFilter<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-rowNodes-forEachNodeAfterFilter" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to forEachNodeAfterFilter property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />

Similar to <code>forEachNode</code>, except skips any filtered out data.

<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />ClientSideRowModelApiModule</a></td>

<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
Function
Similar to <code>forEachNode</code>, except lists all the leaf nodes. This effectively goes through all the data that you provided to the grid before the grid performed any grouping. If using tree data, goes through all the nodes for the data you provided, including nodes that have children, but excluding groups the grid created where gaps were missing in the hierarchy.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/accessing-data/#iterating-rows" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">Iterating Rows<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>

## Selection<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-selection" class="docs-header-icon"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>

<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">selectAll<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-selection-selectAll" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to selectAll property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>

Function
Select all rows. By default this ignores filtering, expansion and pagination settings. Pass the appropriate select all mode as an argument in order to select only rows that satisfy the filter, or those rows on the current page. <code>mode</code>: SelectAll mode to use. See <code>SelectAllMode</code><code>source</code>: Source property that will appear in the <code>selectionChanged</code> event, defaults to <code>'apiSelectAll'</code>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />RowSelectionModule</a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">deselectAll<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-selection-deselectAll" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to deselectAll property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
Function
Clear all row selections. By default this ignores filtering, expansion and pagination settings. Pass the appropriate select all mode as an argument in order to select only rows that satisfy the filter, or those rows on the current page. <code>mode</code>: SelectAll mode to use. See <code>SelectAllMode</code><code>source</code>: Source property that will appear in the <code>selectionChanged</code> event, defaults to <code>'apiSelectAll'</code>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />RowSelectionModule</a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">getSelectedNodes<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-selection-getSelectedNodes" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to getSelectedNodes property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
Function
Returns an unsorted list of selected nodes. Getting the underlying node (rather than the data) is useful when working with tree / aggregated data, as the node can be traversed.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />RowSelectionModule</a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">getSelectedRows<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-selection-getSelectedRows" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to getSelectedRows property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
Function
Returns an unsorted list of selected rows (i.e. row data that you provided).
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />RowSelectionModule</a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">setNodesSelected<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-selection-setNodesSelected" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to setNodesSelected property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
Function
Set all of the provided nodes selection state to the provided value.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />RowSelectionModule</a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">getBestCostNodeSelection<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-selection-getBestCostNodeSelection" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to getBestCostNodeSelection property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
Function
Returns a list of all selected nodes at 'best cost', a feature to be used with groups / trees. If a group has all its children selected, then the group appears in the result, but not the children. Designed for use with <code>'children'</code> as the group selection type, where groups don't actually appear in the selection normally.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />ClientSideRowModelApiModule</a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">getCellRanges<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-selection-getCellRanges" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to getCellRanges property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
Function
Returns the list of selected cell ranges. The start is the first cell the user clicked on and the end is the cell where the user stopped dragging. Do not assume that the start cell's index is numerically before the end cell, as the user could have dragged up.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/cell-selection-api-reference/#reference-selection-getCellRanges" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">getCellRanges<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />CellSelectionModule<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/990149ee91ce979dd318bb1a35da7c14ba75e077.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon _enterpriseIcon_1v1zd_20" /></a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">addCellRange<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-selection-addCellRange" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to addCellRange property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />
Function
Adds the provided cell range to the selected ranges. This keeps any previous ranges. If you wish to only have the new range selected, then call <code>clearCellSelection()</code> first.
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/cell-selection-api-reference/#reference-selection-addCellRange" class="_docLink_1nt5n_359">addCellRange<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/5d3911d58f5e2c7765baa36d9b25aa388d44596b.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/modules/"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/9adc018fe6fa15017f3061d1c905d7f90f4ba7ea.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />CellSelectionModule<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/990149ee91ce979dd318bb1a35da7c14ba75e077.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon _enterpriseIcon_1v1zd_20" /></a></td>
</tr>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">clearCellSelection<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-selection-clearCellSelection" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to clearCellSelection property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>
<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/d9c0dfac54ae9b0d65ccf9f318ddf38d9f0ca75e.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" />

## Sorting<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-sort" class="docs-header-icon"><img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>

<table class="_apiReference_1nt5n_20 _apiReference_119gq_18 no-zebra">
<tbody>
<tr class="_tableRow_119gq_4">
<td class="_propertyNameDescription_119gq_25">onSortChanged<a href="https://www.ag-grid.com/javascript-data-grid/grid-api/#reference-sort-onSortChanged" class="_linkIcon_152wk_1 _docsHeaderIcon_152wk_8 button-secondary _linkIcon_1nt5n_179" aria-label="Link to onSortChanged property">Copy Link<img src="out_ag_grid/grid-api/index_media/76673052bb2634e0af37ce510b283b99cec64e64.svg" class="_icon_1jqgc_1 icon" /></a>

Gets the grid to act as if the sort was changed. Useful if you update some values and want to get the grid to reorder them according to the new values.</td>
</tr>
